            }
        }

        function loadOneTrustScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();

            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color pi-collapse pi-collapse-open">
	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background"><span class="df-header">Devil Fruit</span></h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Nomi_Nomi_no_Mi" title="Nomi Nomi no Mi">Nomi Nomi no Mi</a></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Brain-Brain Fruit</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Brain</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div>
</div>

</section>
</aside>
</p><table class="nomobile dfbox mw-collapsible ScientistColors" style="color: var(--colorscheme-txt, var(--pi-txt-fallback));">
<tbody><tr><th class="cs" style="background: var(--colorscheme-bg, var(--pi-bg-fallback))">Devil Fruit</th></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Nomi_Nomi_no_Mi" title="Nomi Nomi no Mi">Nomi Nomi no Mi</a></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Brain-Brain Fruit</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Brain</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a></div></div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>"Stella" redirects here. For the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Film:_Gold" title="One Piece Film: Gold">One Piece Film: Gold</a> character, see <a href="/wiki/Stella_(Non-Canon)" title="Stella (Non-Canon)">Stella (Non-Canon)</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Dr. Vegapunk</b> was the leading <a href="/wiki/Scientist" title="Scientist">scientist</a> of the <a href="/wiki/SSG" title="SSG">SSG</a> in the employment of the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>. His work included discovering the secrets and uses of <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">seastone</a>, the secrets of how <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> powers work, the co-discovery of the <a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a> and its applications, the creation of the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> and <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a>, and various other scientific achievements that are said to be at least 500 years ahead of current technology.<sup id="cite_ref-c433_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c433-10">[10]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c485_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c485-11">[11]</a></sup> He hailed from the technologically advanced <a href="/wiki/Karakuri_Island" title="Karakuri Island">Karakuri Island</a><sup id="cite_ref-c523_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c523-5">[5]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup> and resided on <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a>, where his laboratory is located.<sup id="cite_ref-Egghead_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Egghead-6">[6]</a></sup>
</p><p>Before being employed under the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, Vegapunk had been the director of an outlaw scientific research team known as <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>, where he worked alongside other notable scientists such as <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Judge" title="Vinsmoke Judge">Vinsmoke Judge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Stussy" title="Buckingham Stussy">Buckingham Stussy</a>. The team was eventually arrested, and Vegapunk was later integrated into the Marines as its head scientist after MADS' dissolution.<sup id="cite_ref-c840_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c840-4">[4]</a></sup> However, once the World Government learned he was researching the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a>, they dispatched <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a> and conspired with his own satellite <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk/York" title="Vegapunk/York">York</a> to eliminate him, which resulted in the monumental <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Incident" title="Egghead Incident">Egghead Incident</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Vegapunk would end up being killed by his old friend, Admiral <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>, during the ensuing <a href="/wiki/Buster_Call" title="Buster Call">Buster Call</a> on Egghead.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> Foreseeing this, however, Vegapunk left behind an important message regarding a catastrophic global future event to be broadcasted around the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a> in the event of his death. <sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup>
</p><p>First mentioned during the <a href="/wiki/Post-Enies_Lobby_Arc" title="Post-Enies Lobby Arc">Post-Enies Lobby Arc</a>, Vegapunk was a major background character throughout the series until his proper introduction during the <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Arc" title="Egghead Arc">Egghead Arc</a>, becoming a major ally to the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> alongside his satellites and playing a central role during its ongoings.
</p>

			<h3 class="trfc161__header-text">Quick Answers</h3>
		</div>
		<img class="trfc161-logo" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/8941553e-df6a-4310-a080-b9da56fdcbdd" alt="fandom logo">
	</div>
	<div class="trfc161__groups">
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8238" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What are some of the scientific achievements of Dr. Vegapunk in One Piece?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Dr. Vegapunk, the scientific genius in One Piece, has made numerous significant contributions. His inventions have had a profound impact on various arcs like Thriller Bark, Sabaody Archipelago, Marineford, Punk Hazard, Whole Cake Island, Wano Country, and Egghead. He's known for his technological advancements for the World Government. His medical expertise is unrivaled, with immense talents in medical biology, including the applications of the Lineage Factor, which gave him great insights into biology and genetics. His work is so influential that even fellow scientist Franky admires him.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8239" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the role of Dr. Vegapunk in the SSG and the Marines?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Dr. Vegapunk plays a pivotal role in the SSG and the Marines as the leader of their scientific research and development team, known as the 'Science Unit'. He is responsible for most of the special technology found in the hands of the Marines, including the innovative use of Seastone lining. Vegapunk's genius has led to him being in charge of several advanced Marine and government facilities, such as Punk Hazard and Egghead. His bodyguard, Sentomaru, acts as the captain of the Science Unit.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8240" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the significance of seastone in Dr. Vegapunk's research?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Seastone plays a pivotal role in Dr. Vegapunk's research. As the leading scientist for the Marines and the World Government, he has conducted the most advanced research on Seastone. His innovations include using Seastone in various inventions and devices, notably among the Marines. One of his significant achievements is the use of Seastone on ship hulls to ward off Sea Kings, enabling safe passage through infested areas like the Calm Belt. Additionally, Vegapunk's team uses Seastone lining on Marine technology, enhancing their capabilities. The full extent of Seastone's properties is still being explored, making it a crucial element in Vegapunk's ongoing research.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8241" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What is the Lineage Factor that Dr. Vegapunk co-discovered?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						The Lineage Factor is a fascinating discovery co-made by Dr. Vegapunk and Vinsmoke Judge. It's the blueprint of life itself, found in all living organisms. This discovery has allowed Dr. Vegapunk to make significant strides in his research, including the creation of artificial lifeforms and the manipulation of Devil Fruit powers. It's also been used in cloning and in creating mindless, emotionless living weapons. Dr. Vegapunk's work with the Lineage Factor is so advanced, it's said to be 500 years ahead of current technology!
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
			<details class="trfc161__group " data-question-id="8242" data-revision-id="2">
				<summary class="trfc161__question-wrapper">
					<b class="trfc161__question">What does Dr. Vegapunk look like in the One Piece series?</b>
						<img class="trfc161__question-chevron" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/835ea5d8-5dd9-4dc6-83dc-8554b30552d7" alt="toggle section">
				</summary>
				<div class="trfc161__answer">
					<div class="quick-answers__answer-text">
						Dr. Vegapunk, the renowned scientist from the One Piece series, is an intriguing character with a unique appearance. He is a relatively tall elderly man, slightly shorter than Jinbe. His body is slender, and he has distinctive red cheeks. Vegapunk's head is elongated and neatly sliced, supported by a shaft that resembles the top of an apple-core and its leaf. His forehead is remarkably wide and his tongue is notably long. This eccentric look perfectly complements his brilliant, yet mysterious persona.
					</div>
					<div class="trfc161__answer-source">
						Provided by: Fandom
					</div>
					<div class="quick_answers__report-module-root" data-reportable="1"></div>
				</div>
			</details>
	</div>
</section>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Satellites">Satellites</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>See also the associated category: <a href="/wiki/Category:Satellites" title="Category:Satellites">Satellites</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p>At some point in the last six years,<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> due to being occupied with his inventions, Vegapunk managed to split his being into six different people, referred to as <b>satellites</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"><ruby lang="ja"><rb>猫</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>サテライト</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby></span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">sateraito</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, kanji literally meaning "cats")</span> or "offshoots"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">分身</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">bunshin</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, which share Vegapunk's brain via <a href="/wiki/Punk_Records" title="Punk Records">Punk Records</a>. These satellites all identify as Dr. Vegapunk and will introduce themselves as such, but also possess their own names and number designations to distinguish them, making them effectively six unique people. The satellites are also distinguished by embodying a particular aspect of Vegapunk's personality.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> Although they all have similar thought patterns,<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> they use different <a href="/wiki/First_Person_Pronoun_Usage" title="First Person Pronoun Usage">first person pronouns</a> and speech patterns. His true body was called the <b>"Stella"</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1062_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1062-7">[7]</a></sup> The method Vegapunk used in order to split his being into six different entities is still unknown. The destruction of a satellite's body does not mean they are killed, as they have countless spare parts to reupload their consciousnesses into.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup>
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Incident" title="Egghead Incident">Egghead Incident</a>, York betrayed Stella and the other satellites,<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup> personally shooting Shaka in the head, and having <a href="/wiki/S-Snake" title="S-Snake">S-Snake</a> crush Pythagoras.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>. Edison was later disconnected from Punk Records while saving <a href="/wiki/Stussy" title="Stussy">Stussy</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> while Atlas detonated herself to ensure that the Straw Hats and Lilith would escape from Egghead.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup> Shaka, Pythagoras, and Atlas survived by reconvening into Edison's body, and the combined Vegapunk rebuilt himself using spare parts.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup> Stella was killed by <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a><sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup>, which did not affect the satellites' survivals.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Vegapunk was a relatively tall elderly man, having stood just under <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> in height (without his brain), with slender limbs and red cheeks. He had a noticeably elongated but neatly sliced head and had a shaft driven in to support a structure resembling the top of an apple-core and its leaf. His forehead was remarkably wide while his eyes were close to his potato nose. His tongue was incredibly long, reaching all the way to his groin, and was always sticking out of his mouth. He had a bald head on top, but had spiky white hair on the sides, as well as a thick mustache. He wore a short white coat with <a href="/wiki/SSG" title="SSG">SSG</a> on the back, a pink shirt with red polka dots, purple pants, and purple DOM shoes. Before he cut out his brain, the size of his head had supposedly reached the height of <a href="/wiki/Giants" title="Giants">giants</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1066_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1066-3">[3]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup>
</p><p>When he was 43 years old, Vegapunk had an enlarged head accounting for much of his height, and his hair was brown and covered most of his head. He wore a leather jacket, a white shirt, a belt, black pants, and dress shoes.
</p><p>Three years ago, Vegapunk created <a href="/wiki/Punk_Records" title="Punk Records">Punk Records</a> and transferred his enlarged brain there to significantly shrink his head.<sup id="cite_ref-c1101_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1101-28">[28]</a></sup>
</p><p>When he was part of <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>, his head was much smaller with a bandage on the left side and lacked the mustache. He wore a Hawaiian shirt and goggles.<sup id="cite_ref-c1070_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1070-29">[29]</a></sup>
</p><p>During <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Kuma</a>'s explanation on his <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> modification, he seemed to be wearing yellow gloves and a striped shirt with a white lab coat.
</p>

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Nomi_Nomi_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240317020525" class="image"><img alt="Nomi Nomi no Mi Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="59" height="140" data-image-name="Nomi Nomi no Mi Infobox.png" data-image-key="Nomi_Nomi_no_Mi_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Nomi_Nomi_no_Mi_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/59?cb=20240317020525" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Vegapunk at age 43.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0e/Vegapunk_At_Age_61.png/revision/latest?cb=20240503071720" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk At Age 61" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="67" height="140" data-image-name="Vegapunk At Age 61.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_At_Age_61.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0e/Vegapunk_At_Age_61.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/67?cb=20240503071720" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Vegapunk at age 61.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fd/Vegapunk%27s_Experiment_Outfit.png/revision/latest?cb=20240519130239" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk's Experiment Outfit" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="98" height="140" data-image-name="Vegapunk's Experiment Outfit.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk%27s_Experiment_Outfit.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fd/Vegapunk%27s_Experiment_Outfit.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/98?cb=20240519130239" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Vegapunk during an experiment with Kuma.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 162px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/Vegapunk_At_Age_62.png/revision/latest?cb=20231211143424" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk At Age 62" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="103" height="140" data-image-name="Vegapunk At Age 62.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_At_Age_62.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/Vegapunk_At_Age_62.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/103?cb=20231211143424" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Vegapunk at age 62.
