</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">He's an odd man, but true to his desires, and trustworthy.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a> on Vegapunk.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[30]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
In his youth, Vegapunk was a generous person who cared very much for the inhabitants of his <a href="/wiki/Karakuri_Island" title="Karakuri Island">island</a>, willing to help them with his inventions. He is considered the island's pride and joy, and the residents are still hoping for his return.
</p><p>Each of Vegapunk's six satellites possesses a dominant personality trait that is presumably present in Vegapunk in general. While he had strong morals and a sense of justice and pride as a scientist (Shaka), he also possessed malevolent traits and an inclination to steal from others in order to fund his research (Lilith) and could be prone to greed and desire (York); there is considerable conflict and reasoning between these two sides. He appeared to be quite thoughtful and wise (Edison and Pythagoras) but could be prone to getting angry at other people's inability to properly replicate and utilize his technological developments, to the point of lashing out violently (Atlas).<sup id="cite_ref-c1062_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1062-7">[7]</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite his many traits, Vegapunk was ultimately a man of great compassion with a strong sense of morality. Much like Dragon, he also despised and lamented the political corruption of the world under the World Govenrment's tyranny, but chose to turn a blind eye to it, using the resources they provided him to further his research for the sake of peace and prosperity for humanity. Due to his compassion, Vegapunk secretly programmed all the Pacifistas to make Bonney the highest authority to prevent a possible tragedy where Bonney, whom Kuma gave his life to protect, ended up getting killed by a fully modified Kuma or his clones by the World Government. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Vegapunk%27s_Dream.png/revision/latest?cb=20240324022022" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk's Dream" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="169" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vegapunk's Dream.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk%27s_Dream.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Vegapunk%27s_Dream.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240324022022"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Vegapunk%27s_Dream.png/revision/latest?cb=20240324022022" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk's Dream" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Vegapunk%27s_Dream.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240324022022" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="169" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vegapunk's Dream.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk%27s_Dream.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/db/Vegapunk%27s_Dream.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240324022022"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vegapunk%27s_Dream.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk shares his ultimate goal of providing free energy to everybody.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Unlike his former fellow MADS scientists <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Judge" title="Vinsmoke Judge">Vinsmoke Judge</a> and <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a>, Vegapunk was far more moral about what he would do in pursuit of scientific achievements. He refused to involve children in the gigantification process despite repeated failures and vetoed the creation or release of the <a href="/wiki/H2S" title="H2S">H2S</a> poison gas weapon for fear of it harming innocent people.<sup id="cite_ref-c684_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c684-1">[1]</a></sup> He also preferred to focus on developing peaceful inventions contrary to the dangerous creations of his former colleagues and was against the idea of converting people into cyborgs like Kuma that included stripping them of their own free will, memories, and emotions comparing this to murder. Likewise, Vegapunk also despised unethical human experimentation and was outraged to learn it was Saturn's experiments that led to the manifestation of the Sapphire Scales on Ginny and Bonney. 
</p><p>Vegapunk had a strongly idealistic and humanitarian side, proudly pronouncing his plans to use his future world-spanning inventions to help humanity and stop ongoing conflicts such as wars, even choosing to work for the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> out of belief he could do more good for people by doing so. Unfortunately, certain people, like <a href="/wiki/Jewelry_Bonney" title="Jewelry Bonney">Jewelry Bonney</a>, fail to see that side of Vegapunk as she was under the belief that he had no qualms with committing sacrifices and atrocities, personal or otherwise, in his aim for greater knowledge and progress. This infamous perception is wrong, as Vegapunk tragically cried when he carried out the order given by Saturn and opposed installing a self-destruct mechanism in Kuma, suggesting applying a device that would give him "two personalities" to give Kuma the opportunity to reunite with his daughter.<sup id="cite_ref-c1102_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1102-31">[31]</a></sup> When Saturn ordered a <a href="/wiki/Buster_Call" title="Buster Call">Buster Call</a> on Egghead, Vegapunk desperately pleaded with the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Elder</a> and Kizaru to reconsider, as destroying Egghead means destroying all the scientific progress made there, which would be a bigger loss to humanity than him personally.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup>
</p><p>He seemed to have an interest for dragons, as he created two of them on <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-dragon1_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dragon1-33">[33]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-dragon2_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dragon2-34">[34]</a></sup> and an <a href="/wiki/Artificial_Devil_Fruit" title="Artificial Devil Fruit">artificial Devil Fruit</a> that allows the user to transform into one.<sup id="cite_ref-c685_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c685-35">[35]</a></sup> However, due to his serious perfectionism, he deemed the fruit a failure since its dragon form was not the same color as the dragon form bestowed by the real Devil Fruit it was based on.<sup id="cite_ref-c1067p7-8_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1067p7-8-36">[36]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Vegapunk_Removes_Kuma_Humanity.png/revision/latest?cb=20231226051642" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Removes Kuma Humanity" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="211" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vegapunk Removes Kuma Humanity.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Removes_Kuma_Humanity.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Vegapunk_Removes_Kuma_Humanity.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231226051642"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Vegapunk_Removes_Kuma_Humanity.png/revision/latest?cb=20231226051642" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Removes Kuma Humanity" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Vegapunk_Removes_Kuma_Humanity.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231226051642" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="211" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vegapunk Removes Kuma Humanity.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Removes_Kuma_Humanity.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Vegapunk_Removes_Kuma_Humanity.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231226051642"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vegapunk_Removes_Kuma_Humanity.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">With a heavy heart, Vegapunk prepares to pull the switch that will take away Kuma's free will.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Given his nature as a scientist, Vegapunk had a natural interest in theories and the nature of science itself. He would elaborate on the works of other scientists if he found them interesting. When he heard that a certain scholar in the West Blue theorized that the human body loses 21 grams if they die, which was the weight of the soul, Vegapunk got so intrigued that he wanted to see it for himself, doing experiments on his thoughts and observing. In addition to the benefits of being an acclaimed scientist, Vegapunk was smart enough aware of the dangers of his job, especially regarding the <a href="/wiki/Ohara_Incident" title="Ohara Incident">Ohara Incident</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a>. Vegapunk considered it a scientist's nature to want to peek at answers, even knowing he had uncovered too much of the past to be kept alive. He knew that <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a> was sent to assassinate him and prevent him from continuing his research.
</p><p>Vegapunk took his survival seriously and did not hesitate to ask for help when necessary. He requested Luffy to get him off Egghead and away from the World Government when they moved to assassinate him, despite just meeting the young <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Emperor</a>. He did not mind dragging others allies into helping him without considering their circumstances first. However, this doesn't mean Vegapunk was a coward who would abandon others to save his own skin and feel no guilt about what would happen to others because of his action. In fact, Vegapunk was willing to put himself in the line of danger to save Bonney after she was knocked down to the Fabiriophase, despite being the Marines' main target.
</p><p>While Vegapunk was a man of science, he was not above believing in things outside of science. He expressed interest in the Sun God Nika and did not deny the possibility of gods being real. After Kuma's miraculous appearance on Egghead in time to save his daughter Bonney from Saturn, despite there being no logical way for the former Warlord to be able to move or even know about his daughter's situation, Vegapunk was so confused by it, but he decided to chalk it up to 'love' and the <a href="/wiki/Buccaneers" title="Buccaneers">Buccaneer</a> race's special power.
</p><p>Vegapunk was also cautious as he knew the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> would attempt to stop his pre-recorded message broadcast. He fooled them by using a <a href="/wiki/Den_Den_Mushi" title="Den Den Mushi">Den Den Mushi</a> as a decoy by disguising it as the Broadcast Den Den Mushi.
</p><p>Vegapunk had shown he was remorseful of the World Government using the <a href="/wiki/Mother_Flame" title="Mother Flame">Mother Flame</a> to power up the Ancient Weapon to destroy <a href="/wiki/Lulusia_Kingdom" title="Lulusia Kingdom">Lulusia Kingdom</a> when he bowed down to apologize to everyone who was watching his recorded message.
</p><p>He had a verbal tic in which he added "Quasar"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">クエーサー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kuēsā</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> to his requests for help.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Satellites_2">Satellites</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3f/Vegapunks_at_work.png/revision/latest?cb=20230916062349" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunks at work" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vegapunks at work.png" data-image-key="Vegapunks_at_work.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3f/Vegapunks_at_work.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230916062349"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3f/Vegapunks_at_work.png/revision/latest?cb=20230916062349" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunks at work" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3f/Vegapunks_at_work.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230916062349" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="138" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vegapunks at work.png" data-image-key="Vegapunks_at_work.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3f/Vegapunks_at_work.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230916062349"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vegapunks_at_work.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk, Edison and Atlas work together to crack York's code.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Vegapunk's satellites all refer to themselves as Vegapunk, they each exemplify only one portion of Vegapunk's personality, and all have their own wills and desires and are therefore effectively six unique people. While this normally isn't an issue as Vegapunk was supposed to synchronize his brain with all of his satellites via <a href="/wiki/Punk_Records" title="Punk Records">Punk Records</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk/York" title="Vegapunk/York">York</a> decided to betray Vegapunk and her fellow satellites in an effort to become a <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Noble</a>. Once her treachery was revealed, she was effectively treated as an enemy by Vegapunk and the other satellites.
</p><p>When it was revealed that one of his satellites was leaking to the World Government his studies in the Void Century, he privately confirmed to Shaka that him and Pythagoras were the only two he trusted without question. Despite this, Vegapunk seemed to be on good terms with all of his Satellites (minus York), as he pre-recorded a message together with Shaka and Pythagoras about the truth of the world all while they conversed about scientific ideas and Vegapunk shared a coffee with them, even all of them jokingly spending the time when Vegapunk burned his tongue on the coffee, with Pythagoras worried and Shaka knowing it had that effect.  
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Vegapunk was once arrested by the World Government for his dangerous experiments in relation to research conducted into the <a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">cloning</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c840_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c840-4">[4]</a></sup> Despite this run in with the bureaucracy, he was employed as their chief scientist in the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>. He would go onto becoming the leader of the <a href="/wiki/SSG" title="SSG">SSG</a>.
</p><p>Despite being of great help in drastically increasing the Marines' military might with his inventions of the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> and <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a>, among presumably other things, the World Government has elected to kill him, which <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a> was sent on a mission to do, due to the fear he might perceive too much about the truth.<sup id="cite_ref-c1062_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1062-7">[7]</a></sup> Their fear was proven correct, as Vegapunk had studied all the books the scholars of Ohara had saved during the <a href="/wiki/Ohara_Incident" title="Ohara Incident">Ohara Incident</a> and learned about the Ancient Kingdom. Understanding what the higher-ups would do were they to discover this, Vegapunk chose to keep it a secret, never revealing to them that Ohara had success in protecting their prized books. Vegapunk does not seem to view the World Government in a positive light, admitting to the Straw Hats he completely used all of the funding given for his inventions and only joining them to further his own research endeavors. 
</p><p>Having seen the horrid ways of the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a>, Vegapunk was disgusted by them and was shocked that York would want to become one of them.<sup id="cite_ref-c1078_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1078-38">[38]</a></sup>
</p><p>Vegapunk cared about the staff that worked on Egghead. He never told any of them about his research into the Void Century so they wouldn't be treated as criminals should the World Government find out. He was horrified and outraged that Saturn ordered the ship carrying all the escape staff to be destroyed on the possibility that someone on board knew something.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Jaygarcia_Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Vegapunk_And_Saturn_Argue.png/revision/latest?cb=20231226051653" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk And Saturn Argue" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="193" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vegapunk And Saturn Argue.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_And_Saturn_Argue.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Vegapunk_And_Saturn_Argue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231226051653"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Vegapunk_And_Saturn_Argue.png/revision/latest?cb=20231226051653" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk And Saturn Argue" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Vegapunk_And_Saturn_Argue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231226051653" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="193" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vegapunk And Saturn Argue.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_And_Saturn_Argue.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Vegapunk_And_Saturn_Argue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231226051653"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vegapunk_And_Saturn_Argue.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk fearlessly argues with Saturn.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Vegapunk seemed to display a particularly antagonistic relationship with Saint <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a>. While they originally met on positive terms when Vegapunk was welcomed to <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a> for winning the Ibel Peace Prize, that was where their cordiality ended, when Vegapunk witnessed the deplorable behavior of the World Nobles. Vegapunk and Saturn had argued on at least two separate occasions on the subject of the unethical nature of Kuma's conversion into a human weapon. The two seemed to have a mutual disrespect for one another, with Vegapunk fearlessly arguing with Saturn, whilst Saturn rejected Vegapunk's concerns and reminded him of his place. Saturn would eventually order Vegapunk's death for studying the Void Century, and went to Egghead, where he confronted Vegapunk personally.<sup id="cite_ref-c1100_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1100-40">[40]</a></sup> When those meet in-person, they were hostile. Vegapunk was even more infuriated when he learned about Saturn’s actions that made Kuma’s life to be tragic for ruining his loved ones’ life. When realizing Kuma's self-destruction mechanism is not working, Saturn demanded Vegapunk if this was his doing, which he confirmed because he didn't install it to Kuma. Upon this, Saturn dubbed Vegapunk a traitor. When Saturn questioned Vegapunk on how Kuma was still able to retain his free will and attack him, Vegapunk cheekily told him the "power of love" was the answer. When Saturn learned of Vegapunk's secret betrayal by programming the Kuma-based Pacifista to obey Jewelry Bonney above all others, he furiously stabbed Vegapunk.<br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Sentomaru" title="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</a> was a young boy, Vegapunk saved him, thus Sentomaru considers Vegapunk's safety as a personal debt. However, Vegapunk does mention this debt as a way to pressure Sentomaru into swaying his loyalty from the Marines to him.<sup id="cite_ref-c1069_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1069-41">[41]</a></sup> Since then, Sentomaru served as his bodyguard, before becoming a Marine officer in between the timeskip. <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk/Shaka" title="Vegapunk/Shaka">Shaka</a> trusts his abilities and allegiance enough to put three <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a> under his command when <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a> invaded <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1068_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1068-42">[42]</a></sup> Vegapunk was deeply saddened to see Sentomaru struck down in order to help him escape, openly crying after Kizaru defeated him.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup>
</p><p>Sentomaru called Vegapunk "Old Man Punk".
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kizaru">Kizaru</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Vegapunk was acquainted with <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Borsalino</a> in his younger days as a Marine cadet as, while on a mission to a village to deal with a bear problem, they encountered a young Sentomaru who defeated the bears and requested to be Vegapunk's bodyguard and to be trained by Borsalino. The three of them became close as Borsalino agreed to use his <a href="/wiki/Pika_Pika_no_Mi" title="Pika Pika no Mi">Devil Fruit ability</a> for Vegapunk to study for a future <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">project</a> and to entertain Sentomaru. As the years went by and with Borsalino eventually becoming an admiral, their relationship soured, with Vegapunk being more apprehensive towards him after he brought a Marine fleet to surround Egghead under orders, with Vegapunk claiming he hates this side of Borsalino the most, even bluntly telling him to shut up when he defended the suggestion of turning Kuma into a human weapon. Despite this, they were still on relatively good enough terms that he was seen eating and partying with Vegapunk and Sentomaru while Kuma and Bonney where at his lab. 
</p><p>Three and a half years later, the World Government deemed Vegapunk a threat and had sent Kizaru to kill him, to which he obliged with some reservations. Vegapunk, fully aware of how strong Kizaru is, held fear of and panicked when he managed to break into the Labophase to confront him. Kizaru has admitted to Vegapunk that having to kill an old friend isn't easy for him. Vegapunk had voiced his disgust at Kizaru labelling him a sad man, to which the Admiral does not deny and wishes he brought darker sunglasses. Tragically, Kizaru would be the one to deal the final strike that led to Vegapunk's death, ultimately showing their former friendship was not enough to convince Kizaru to turn away from his mission. Despite this, Kizaru was still conflicted about this, as when Fleet Admiral Sakazuki warned him about "better not have done a sloppy job", Kizaru asked the fleet admiral if he ever killed a close friend and angrily and tearfully retorted that if Sakazuki got time to doubt his job, he should come and see his work for himself.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fujitora">Fujitora</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Vegapunk seemed to be amicable to the newly promoted <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a>. He revealed a <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">new invention</a> to <a href="/wiki/Issho" title="Issho">Fujitora</a> that could lead to the abolishment of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a> system.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Caesar_Clown">Caesar Clown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite once being colleagues, Vegapunk and <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> had a bitter rivalry based on levels of recognition and ethics. When Caesar's erratic behavior got out of hand, Vegapunk decided to dismiss Caesar from his position. Caesar was also considered second best to Vegapunk. Because of this, Caesar held a grudge against him.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[45]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c684_1-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c684-1">[1]</a></sup> Vegapunk also looked down on some of Caesar's achievements, such as considering the <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILEs</a> to be unacceptable.<sup id="cite_ref-c1070_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1070-29">[29]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bartholomew_Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240512020453" class="image"><img alt="Kuma &amp; Vegapunk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma &amp; Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240512020453"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240512020453" class="image"><img alt="Kuma &amp; Vegapunk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240512020453" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma &amp; Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cc/Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240512020453"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_%26_Vegapunk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk and Kuma.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Vegapunk met <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> when he came looking for a cure for his <a href="/wiki/Jewelry_Bonney" title="Jewelry Bonney">daughter</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sapphire_Scales" title="Sapphire Scales">disease</a>. After learning he was a <a href="/wiki/Buccaneers" title="Buccaneers">Buccaneer</a>, Vegapunk offered to cure Bonney for free in exchange for participating in his cloning project,<sup id="cite_ref-c1099_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1099-46">[46]</a></sup> but he kept this a secret from whoever would be interested in that information. When <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a> gave Vegapunk orders to erase all of Kuma's free will and memories, he was visibly angered by these demands and initially attempted to refuse them, only relenting because Kuma accepted these terms in an effort to protect Bonney, moving the doctor to tears. Over the next two years, Vegapunk and Kuma grew closer as friends while he conducted several experiments on him, including one where the latter was requested to materialize his memories through his own Devil Fruit abilities for Vegapunk to study. While Kuma at first refused, he eventually complied and allowed Vegapunk access to his now tangible memories. Vegapunk, out of respect, kept Kuma's memories locked up inside a high-security room within his laboratory.<sup id="cite_ref-c1072_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1072-47">[47]</a></sup> 
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Your death is a nuisance.. to every person who's ever known and loved you!!! Listen to me, Kuma... and listen good! YOU ARE A HERO!!! TO BONNEY!!! AND TO US ALL!!!<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup></td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
When the time came to remove Kuma's free will, Vegapunk tried to reason with Saturn to allow him bare minimum will power causing the elder to refuse telling the scientist to remove all of his will on top of applying a self-destruct switch into him. Kuma hearing this asked Vegapunk to pass on a message to his daughter, telling her to have a happy tenth birthday, and to grant him his final wish as a human being, which was to program Kuma to protect the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> until the Straw Hats returned.<sup id="cite_ref-c603_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c603-49">[49]</a></sup> Before completing the operation, Vegapunk told Kuma he was a hero for his efforts to Bonney and many others for his sacrifices throughout his life completely breaking down in tears as he pulled the switch to erase Kuma's will.<sup id="cite_ref-c1102_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1102-31">[31]</a></sup> When Kuma arrived in time to save Bonney from Saturn, he was left confused on how that was possible as it defied logic and reasoning due to his memories being erased and the shutdown switch that was activated by Saturn, coming to the conclusion it must be due to his <a href="/wiki/Buccaneers" title="Buccaneers">Buccaneer heritage</a>. Seeing Kuma is unable to move due to his injuries, Vegapunk ordered <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk/Atlas" title="Vegapunk/Atlas">Atlas</a> to carry him. His undying respect for Kuma's bond with Bonney led him to secretly programmed Kuma's Pacifista clones to make Bonney the highest authority to prevent a possible tragedy where Bonney whom Kuma sacrifice everything to protect is killed by the Pacifista.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Vegapunk seemed to have an interest in the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> because he learned from Kuma prior to losing his humanity about Luffy being Dragon's son and having similarities to Nika, as he saw no issue with granting the latter his final wish as a human to protect the group's ship, the Thousand Sunny, until a member of the crew returned for it. He fulfilled Kuma's last wish and programmed him to protect the ship for two entire years, despite his long-established history and connection to the Marines and to the World Government as a whole. One of his "satellites", Shaka even expressed an interest in meeting them after they appeared on the island of <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1062_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1062-7">[7]</a></sup> Also, at least one part of his other interest in the Straw Hats stems from Nico Robin and her past as the only survivor of the <a href="/wiki/Ohara_Incident" title="Ohara Incident">Ohara Incident</a>, as Shaka was seen discussing the full scale as well as the aftermath of the Ohara Incident with Robin, revealing crucial information about the survival of the former <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_D._Saul" title="Jaguar D. Saul">Jaguar D. Saul</a>, the safekeeping of all books of Ohara, his own study of every single book and thus his extended knowledge about the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a>. Though he acknowledged them as pirates, he was shown to have enough trust in the Straw Hats to discuss and reveal important information about the Void Century as well as his own knowledge about it to the group, even ignoring their refusal to listen to such jeopardizing information. He was also not shy of indulging into his own past, which included his relationship with <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>, Luffy's father and leader of the Revolutionary Army, much to the surprise of the Straw Hats.
</p><p>Later, when he saw Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_5_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 5 Techniques">awakened form</a> for the first time, he was stunned about its existence, questioning the Straw Hats if they knew what that form was. He would then explain to them what he knew about this form as being the <a href="/wiki/Nika" title="Nika">Sun God Nika</a>, once again leaving them surprised. He even went as far as sharing his theories about why Devil Fruits were created with the Straw Hats, showing he had enough trust in them to share what he knew about human's most desires, as he was putting it.
</p><p>When the Stella Vegapunk later encountered Luffy's group, he immediately recognized Luffy as the son of <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a> and asked him to take him away from Egghead. Vegapunk would explain his ultimate goal as well his background to the group, putting enough trust into them though he had just met them. He would even fall into funny interactions with Luffy about his extraordinary knowledge and Luffy's seemingly disinterest in such matters. His trust would go to such lengths as that he was considering Luffy and the Straw Hats the only people capable of taking him away from Egghead and keeping him safe from the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>'s clutches, a mutual feeling that was shared by Luffy who agreed to take Vegapunk with them. Vegapunk's faith in Luffy's abilities is strengthen by him being the Sun God Nika, believing even a Buster Call is a trivial problem for him.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>, being a fellow scientist with a passion for creativity, is a huge admirer of Vegapunk since reading his notes on <a href="/wiki/Karakuri_Island" title="Karakuri Island">Baldimore</a> and is increasingly impressed upon meeting the scientist (and his satellites) in person. <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> and <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>, however, are more wary of him despite their impression on his genius, due to his inventions being a potential threat towards them and pirates in general. Nami vehemently objected bringing Vegapunk and his satellites with them on their ship because she does not want to deal the potential problems of doing so, despite the many advantages of having the world's smartest person as an ally. <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Robin</a> is grateful to Vegapunk for protecting Ohara's legacy and revealing to her that her <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_D._Saul" title="Jaguar D. Saul">old friend</a> she thought was dead was actually alive. Chopper is greatly impressed by many of Vegapunk's inventions, especially his medical purpose ones.
</p><p>When Vegapunk went missing, Luffy and Chopper were searching for him, as the crew would not leave <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a> without him. Luffy and his allies freed Vegapunk from his captured and detained <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk/York" title="Vegapunk/York">York</a>. Later, when Vegapunk tragically died, Sanji would carry (unknowingly) his already dead body with him, not leaving him behind and still hoping Vegapunk would get up, all while protecting him from any harm incoming. After escaping Egghead, Sanji mourns for Vegapunk when he couldn't save him. Before he passed on, Vegapunk expressed to Sanji his dying wish for him and his crew to be the ones to ultimately find the One Piece, showing the utmost faith he has on leaving the fate of the world up to them. Luffy cries for Vegapunk while eating after he couldn't save him despite their promise.
</p><p>Luffy called Vegapunk as "Old Man Apple" and like Sentomaru, he also called Vegapunk as "Old Man Punk".
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Vegapunk had a cordial relationship with <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>, the Revolutionary. Though Vegapunk shares Dragon's contempt with the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>'s corruption, he did not join the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a> when Dragon invited him, as he deemed the army to be poor. Regardless, the two shared their respect for <a href="/wiki/Clou_D._Clover" title="Clou D. Clover">Professor Clover</a> and worked to ensure the famous <a href="/wiki/Archaeologist" title="Archaeologist">archaeologist</a>'s death will not be in vain.<sup id="cite_ref-c1066_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1066-3">[3]</a></sup> Also, those two do keep in contact with each other as it was Dragon who recommended the scientist to Kuma, who was looking for a cure for Jewelry Bonney.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Clou_D._Clover">Clou D. Clover</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Vegapunk was a friend of the famous archaeologist <a href="/wiki/Clou_D._Clover" title="Clou D. Clover">Clou D. Clover</a>, and one of the few people to know his true name.<sup id="cite_ref-c1120_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1120-50">[50]</a></sup> He was devastated when the Government launched a <a href="/wiki/Buster_Call" title="Buster Call">Buster Call</a> and propaganda against <a href="/wiki/Ohara" title="Ohara">Ohara</a> for their research of the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a>, and paid tribute to the lives lost there by placing flowers. Despite his earlier hesitation on the subject,<sup id="cite_ref-c1120_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1120-50">[50]</a></sup> Vegapunk also went to <a href="/wiki/Elbaph" title="Elbaph">Elbaph</a> to read the library of books that the <a href="/wiki/New_Giant_Warrior_Pirates" title="New Giant Warrior Pirates">New Giant Warrior Pirates</a> retrieved and saved, intending to continue Clover's research and legacy.<sup id="cite_ref-c1066_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1066-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jewelry_Bonney">Jewelry Bonney</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 138px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Bonney_Hugs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240107060213" class="image"><img alt="Bonney Hugs Vegapunk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="138" height="183" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bonney Hugs Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Bonney_Hugs_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Bonney_Hugs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/138?cb=20240107060213"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Bonney_Hugs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240107060213" class="image"><img alt="Bonney Hugs Vegapunk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Bonney_Hugs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/138?cb=20240107060213" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="138" height="183" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bonney Hugs Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Bonney_Hugs_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fc/Bonney_Hugs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/138?cb=20240107060213"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bonney_Hugs_Vegapunk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Bonney forgiving Vegapunk</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Vegapunk knew <a href="/wiki/Jewelry_Bonney" title="Jewelry Bonney">Bonney</a> since she was a child. However, Bonney held a grudge against him for turning her father Kuma into a mindless <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">cyborg</a>, and upon meeting him, she threatened to kill him and demanded that he change her father back to normal, it was then unknown that Vegapunk would act in rebellion against Saturn by turning Kuma into a cyborg without conscience. Vegapunk has shown to understand the reason why Bonney held a grudge against him and wished to do something for her. After learning the truth, her resentment toward Vegapunk was redirected to Saturn.
</p><p>Vegapunk greatly cared about Bonney's safety, putting her life and safety above his own. He especially worried about what would happen if Bonney, being a pirate, end up encountering a <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> or worse, her own father Kuma. Not wanting to see Bonney getting killed by a clone of her beloved father or Kuma killing his beloved daughter, Vegapunk secretly gave Bonney the highest authority over the Pacifista.<br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Stussy">Stussy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Stussy" title="Stussy">Stussy</a> is the first successful <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">clone</a> that Vegapunk and <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a> managed to create.<sup id="cite_ref-Stussy_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stussy-51">[51]</a></sup> She was loyal to Vegapunk, and despite serving as a spy in the World Government for him for over two decades, she was awaiting for his orders to help him even if it meant betraying <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup> She mentions to have visited <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a> in the past.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup> Stussy would protect Vegapunk from Rob Lucci, using herself as a human shield.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Being held in regard by most of the world as the world's smartest man due to his natural genius intellect and Devil Fruit, Vegapunk had contributed to numerous technological developments and was seen as one of the most notable figures in the world. Vegapunk was notable for having formerly led <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>, a rogue research team involved in several scientific discoveries and development of weapons. After this, he began working for the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> and became one of their scientists, holding a very high position within the organization as one of their leading scientific authorities for several years. Vegapunk was in charge of a number of highly advanced Marine and government facilities, such as <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a> and <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a>. He was the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>' scientific research and development team, The "Science Unit" (科学部隊, Kagaku Butai?) which is responsible for most of the special technology found in the hands of Marines, including, for example, the use of <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a> lining on Marine battleships, which allows those to cross the <a href="/wiki/Calm_Belt" title="Calm Belt">Calm Belt</a> without disturbing the resident <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea Kings</a>. Another major achievement of this unit consists of the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> project.
</p><p>In addition to the normal Science Unit of the Marines, Vegapunk was in charge of the <a href="/wiki/SSG" title="SSG">SSG</a>, the special science division, which provided advanced technology and weaponry for the World Government, including not only the Pacifista, but also the <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a>, which the Government hoped would be able to replace the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords</a> system as one of the current <a href="/wiki/Three_Great_Powers" title="Three Great Powers">Three Great Powers</a>. As the lead Scientist of both units, Vegapunk was in charge of every other scientist and researcher on the island of <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a>, with this authority being shared with his Satellites, who split his workload and responsibilities equally with him in order for him to focus on new innovations. As the creator of the Pacifista and Seraphim, Vegapunk has command over all of them, and is able to give them orders of any kind as a result, with his authority being the third highest, being shared with his satellites and being overruled only by the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> themselves, who lead the World Government, and Jewelry Bonney, who he secretly put her as the highest authority. 
</p><p>After the discovery of his research into the Void Century, Vegapunk was stripped of his authority within the World Government and Marines and was considered to be a security risk for the organization, so much so that the Five Elders ordered his assassination despite his importance and worth to the World Government.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Scientific_Expertise">Scientific Expertise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>While it is unclear when Vegapunk started using his satellites to split his workload, he himself is famed as the greatest scientific genius the world has ever known, having tremendous knowledge and unmatched understanding in all fields of science, from cell biology to military technology, at the beginning of his work on <a href="/wiki/Karakuri_Island" title="Karakuri Island">Karakuri Island</a> as noted by <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>. His scientific expertise is said to be at least 500 years ahead of his contemporaries.<sup id="cite_ref-c485_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c485-11">[11]</a></sup> It seems that even in his youth, the scientist was a prodigy already considered a genius, but lacked the skills, funds, and materials to develop his inventions, although that did not stop him from theorizing the creation of <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">cyborgs</a>, including their laser weapons back then. This is proven by the fact that Franky was able to recreate the technologies by studying the blueprints Vegapunk left behind on his home island. Regardless, the creations and blueprints that he has left behind are considered invaluable, and any damage inflicted to them is considered a crime.<sup id="cite_ref-Nightmare_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nightmare-56">[56]</a></sup> The lasers that are installed into the Pacifista were apparently supposed to be so advanced, that only Vegapunk knew how to create them. It was also stated that the dragons found on Punk Hazard were Vegapunk's own creations.
</p><p>Vegapunk had a deep knowledge and understanding of <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruits</a>, having studied many old texts about them. He was the only known person beside the Five Elders to realize the <a href="/wiki/Nika" title="Nika">true nature</a> of Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi">Devil Fruit</a> after witnessing his <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_5_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 5 Techniques">awakened form</a>. He discovered exactly how Devil Fruit powers are transferred over to a user, and he was also the scientist behind the method of adding Devil Fruit powers into inanimate objects, such as swords and guns.<sup id="cite_ref-seastone_bottom_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-seastone_bottom-57">[57]</a></sup> By using this method, he was able to create a unique blood for his latest creation, the <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a>, by extracting the Lineage Factor of a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a> User, synthesizing it, creating the so-called "<a href="/wiki/Green_Blood" title="Green Blood">Green Blood</a>". He even went as far as having developed a theory about how Devil Fruits came into existence from his knowledge, theorizing that Devil Fruits are the embodiment of what humans desire and could become, which is also the reason why the sea, which he calls "the mother of nature" rejects any Devil Fruit user and makes them unable to swim, as such behavior is loathed by the sea and it considers these wishes to transcend the world people wish to live in as "abnormalities".<sup id="cite_ref-c1069_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1069-41">[41]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tactical_Skills">Tactical Skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Vegapunk was very cunning and deceptive when he needed to be, despite York saying he was a terrible actor and liar. For over 20 years, he researched the Void Century while working for the World Government without them noticing. In fact, the only reason the Five Elders were able to discover his treachery was because one of Vegapunk's <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk/York" title="Vegapunk/York">own satellites</a> betrayed him. Once he found about York's betrayal, Veagpunk (along with Shaka, and Pythagoras) had set up plans to make sure his death would not be in vain and would have the worst consequence for the World Government.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup> Vegapunk was also very skilled at hiding certain functions of some of his devices without others noticing.
</p><p>Vegapunk also possessed impressive intuition, often correctly understanding the truth without solid evidence.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Medical_Expertise">Medical Expertise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Vegapunk was an unrivaled medical genius, aided by his immense talents in medical biology including the applications of the <a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a>, which gave him great insights into biology and genetics, to the point of being able to perfectly create <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">Cyborgs</a> with partially or fully integrated bodies, create <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">clones</a>, and even out right produce artificial life. He was the one who modified <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> into a cyborg,<sup id="cite_ref-c485_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c485-11">[11]</a></sup> and he has produced many <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> replicas of him as well, granting them some of the abilities of <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Pika_Pika_no_Mi" title="Pika Pika no Mi">Devil Fruit</a> in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-Pacifistas_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pacifistas-59">[59]</a></sup> These replicas bleed actual blood, like Kuma himself. However, they lack Kuma's own <a href="/wiki/Nikyu_Nikyu_no_Mi" title="Nikyu Nikyu no Mi">Devil Fruit</a> abilities. After the two-year timeskip, <a href="/wiki/Sentomaru" title="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</a> revealed that the latest Pacifista had been further modified;<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup> these were later revealed to be the <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a>, replicas of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a> in their youth, albeit with <a href="/wiki/Lunarians" title="Lunarians">Lunarian</a> traits.<sup id="cite_ref-c1059_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1059-61">[61]</a></sup> As noted by Chopper, Vegapunk also pioneer organ culture, the science of cultivation of either whole organs or parts of organs in vitro. Vegapunk also developed stem cell therapy which he used to cure Bonney of Sapphire Scales which is considered incurable by his contemporary doctors.
</p><p>Perhaps Vegapunk's greatest medical feat is surgically removing his own giant head and part of his brain without killing himself. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Engineering_Expertise">Engineering Expertise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Vegapunk was a tremendously talented inventor, engineer and mechanic whose genius has allowed him to specialize and produce the creation of multiple inventions and technology so advanced, that it's been stated that it would take the rest of the world 500 years to keep up with him and his inventions. His skill is great enough to be able to develop a number of cutting-edge technologies, such as <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">Cyborgs</a> and Robots. In his early years, he was responsible for turning his homeland of <a href="/wiki/Karakuri_Island" title="Karakuri Island">Karakuri Island</a> into a technological marvel, with the island being known as the "Future Island" for its tech and was responsible for turning a majority of the wildlife on the island into a Cyborg workforce to help build a lot of the tech that the island was known for. As the leading scientist of the World Government and Marines, Vegapunk was responsible for the creation of a lot of the technological advancements that they actively deploy, namely <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a>-covered battleships and equipment, and also various weapons from traditional military weaponry, to living weapons like the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a>. Just like with <a href="/wiki/Karakuri_Island" title="Karakuri Island">Karakuri Island</a>, Vegapunk turned the island of <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a> into a "Future Island" with a wide variety of advanced technology stemming from climate altering tech, to holograms and mechanized wildlife, to machines that automatically produce clothing and food, to even a state of the art lab facility built on top of artificially created <a href="/wiki/Sea_Clouds" title="Sea Clouds">Sea</a> and <a href="/wiki/Island_Clouds" title="Island Clouds">Island</a> clouds with advanced security. Like his early blueprints and creations, Vegapunk's many inventions on Egghead are immensely invaluable, with the destruction of any of them being a considerable loss for the World Government.<sup id="cite_ref-c1062_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1062-7">[7]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Oceanography">Oceanography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Via his research, he discovered ways of allowing <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ships" title="Marine Ships">Marine ships</a> to pass through the <a href="/wiki/Calm_Belt" title="Calm Belt">Calm Belts</a> without fear of a <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea King</a> attack, by covering the bottom of the ships with <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Archaeology">Archaeology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Continuing Clover's research to honor his memory, Vegapunk has read and fully memorized every single book that had been rescued from Ohara. He was able to uncover many secrets from the Void Century and read the Poneglyphs which led the Five Elders to order his assassination for knowing too much.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Nomi_Nomi_no_Mi" title="Nomi Nomi no Mi">Nomi Nomi no Mi</a></i></dd></dl>
<p>Vegapunk ate the Nomi Nomi no Mi, a <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allowed his brain to store an indefinite amount of information and eidetically recall everything he has ever learned. It also caused his brain and head to expand continuously as he acquires new knowledge.<sup id="cite_ref-c1067p2-5_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1067p2-5-62">[62]</a></sup> While Vegapunk was already a natural genius, the Nomi Nomi no Mi absolutely enhanced his mental efficiency and aptitude for learning and research such as his scientific genius which is unparalleled compared to the rest of the world, making futuristic breakthrough in science and technology by at least five hundred years.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Satellites_3">Satellites</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Due to splitting himself up into six people, Vegapunk was able to be many times more productive as his satellites are capable of working independently at the same time. The fact that each of his satellites can also be equipped with weapons, vehicles, and technology also made Vegapunk drastically more difficult to handle in combat. The satellites are capable of communicating with each other via an earpiece and may also share senses as Shaka was able to see what was around <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk/Lilith" title="Vegapunk/Lilith">Lilith</a> while the two of them were in different locations.<sup id="cite_ref-c1062_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1062-7">[7]</a></sup> Necessary bodily functions can be assigned to one satellite, allowing the others to forgo them. Currently, <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk/York" title="Vegapunk/York">York</a> is tasked with eating, sleeping, urinating, and defecating on behalf of the rest of the satellites.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup> One of the only downsides to Vegapunk splitting himself up into six people, is that the satellites have just as much free will and independent thought as the original Vegapunk, and are more than capable of thinking and doing things for their own self interests. York secretly had the ambition to become a Celestial Dragon, was not only prepared to betray her fellow Vegapunks, but even orchestrate multiple events and leak information directly to the World Government about Vegapunk's research, all in order to have Vegapunk and the other Satellites killed so the World Government would grant her wish of becoming a Celestial Dragon.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Scientific_Achievements">Scientific Achievements</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
