</th></tr>
<tr>
<td>Creating living weapons
</td>
<td><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Vegapunk%27s_Research.png/revision/latest?cb=20220927023708" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk's Research" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" data-image-name="Vegapunk's Research.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk%27s_Research.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/09/Vegapunk%27s_Research.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220927023708" class="lazyload"></a>
</td>
<td>Enabling inanimate objects to "eat" fruits and gain their powers.<sup id="cite_ref-Devil_Fruits_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Devil_Fruits-70">[70]</a></sup>
</td>
<td>Vegapunk
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>Replicating Devil Fruit powers
</td>
<td><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png/revision/latest?cb=20230124051021" class="image"><img alt="Kuma Fires A Laser Beam" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" data-image-name="Kuma Fires A Laser Beam.png" data-image-key="Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Kuma_Fires_A_Laser_Beam.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230124051021" class="lazyload"></a>
</td>
<td>Artificially replicate Devil Fruit powers for other weapons (namely, developing <a href="/wiki/Laser" title="Laser">lasers</a> by researching the mechanics of the <a href="/wiki/Pika_Pika_no_Mi" title="Pika Pika no Mi">Pika Pika no Mi</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-Pacifistas_59-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pacifistas-59">[59]</a></sup>
</td>
<td>Vegapunk
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>The science of Devil Fruits
</td>
<td><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Artificial_Devil_Fruit_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230211084451" class="image"><img alt="Artificial Devil Fruit Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" data-image-name="Artificial Devil Fruit Infobox.png" data-image-key="Artificial_Devil_Fruit_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Artificial_Devil_Fruit_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230211084451" class="lazyload"></a>
</td>
<td>He discovered that <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruits</a> alter the Lineage Factors of their consumers,<sup id="cite_ref-Devil_Fruits_70-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Devil_Fruits-70">[70]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[71]</a></sup> and utilized <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>'s Lineage Factor to create an <a href="/wiki/Artificial_Devil_Fruit" title="Artificial Devil Fruit">artificial replica</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu</a>. It was labeled a failure,<sup id="cite_ref-c685_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c685-35">[35]</a></sup> solely due the incorrect coloration of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Momonosuke</a>'s Dragon form,<sup id="cite_ref-c1067p7-8_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1067p7-8-36">[36]</a></sup> and so its consumer has managed to manifest many of the same abilities.
</td>
<td>Vegapunk
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Green_Blood" title="Green Blood">Green Blood</a>
</td>
<td><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Green_Blood_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240421020919" class="image"><img alt="Green Blood Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" data-image-name="Green Blood Infobox.png" data-image-key="Green_Blood_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Green_Blood_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240421020919" class="lazyload"></a>
</td>
<td>A substance created from the Lineage Factor of Paramecia-type Devil Fruit users, in order to replicate those fruits abilities.
