<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Vegapunk was born 65 years ago in the Future Country Baldimore on <a href="/wiki/Karakuri_Island" title="Karakuri Island">Karakuri Island</a>. As a child, he designed and built several devices in his lab, including <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">robotic animals</a>. He also had hundreds of other ideas, ranging from weapons to experimenting with cellular structures. He once tried to create an in-ground heating system for the island's people using modified animals as his labor force. Unfortunately, Vegapunk lacked the tools and the funds needed to complete his project, but he was able to touch the people's hearts.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">[92]</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point, Vegapunk ate the <a href="/wiki/Nomi_Nomi_no_Mi" title="Nomi Nomi no Mi">Nomi Nomi no Mi</a>, which caused his brain and head to expand continuously as he acquired new knowledge.<sup id="cite_ref-c1067p2-5_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1067p2-5-62">[62]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest?cb=20230919224736" class="image"><img alt="MADS Members" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="235" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="MADS Members.png" data-image-key="MADS_Members.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230919224736"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest?cb=20230919224736" class="image"><img alt="MADS Members" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230919224736" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="235" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="MADS Members.png" data-image-key="MADS_Members.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9a/MADS_Members.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230919224736"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:MADS_Members.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk as part of MADS.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>39 years ago, Vegapunk became one of the founding members of the illegal research team, <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a>, working alongside <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Judge" title="Vinsmoke Judge">Vinsmoke Judge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Queen" title="Queen">Queen</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Stussy" title="Buckingham Stussy">Buckingham Stussy</a>. While the other scientists focused on creating weapons,<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">[93]</a></sup> Vegapunk pursued peace-promoting products, like the GP Flowers which earned him the Ibel Peace Prize.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">[94]</a></sup> This led to the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> inviting Vegapunk to meet them in <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">[95]</a></sup> 36 years ago, Vegapunk also discovered the <a href="/wiki/Lineage_Factor" title="Lineage Factor">Lineage Factor</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c840_4-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c840-4">[4]</a></sup> and that same year MADS team successfully created a <a href="/wiki/Cloning" title="Cloning">clone</a> of Stussy.<sup id="cite_ref-Stussy_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Stussy-51">[51]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">[96]</a></sup>
</p><p>26 years ago, the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> felt threatened by Vegapunk's discoveries and experiments, especially those tied to Lineage Factor, and ordered his arrest through <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Borsalino</a>. though Vegapunk brushed off the "arrest" and instead questioned him about the monetary funds he would eventually receive for his research projects, knowing full well that the Marines were in fact interested in having him within their ranks. Borsalino found this amusing and became friends with Vegapunk soon after.<sup id="cite_ref-c1124_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1124-97">[97]</a></sup> MADS was subsequently dissolved, or rather, absorbed, with Vegapunk and <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> joining the government's research team.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Service_to_the_World_Government">Service to the World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After going to work for the World Government, Vegapunk became famous for his <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> research and for discovering that <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">Seastone</a> can counteract the effects of Devil Fruit on the user.<sup id="cite_ref-c433_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c433-10">[10]</a></sup> In that same year, Vegapunk met with <a href="/wiki/Clou_D._Clover" title="Clou D. Clover">Clou D. Clover</a> at the entrance to Punk Hazard, with Clover requesting Vegapunk's assistance in researching the Void Century. Due to the heavy risk presented from such a task, Vegapunk denied helping. Upon hearing of the death of Clover's brother as a result of his name, Vegapunk remained adamant with his initial decision, although he agreed to remain silent on the matter.<sup id="cite_ref-c1120_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1120-50">[50]</a></sup>
</p><p>Vegapunk worked with a sample of Kaidou's Lineage Factor, extracted from him when he was captured in Punk Hazard, to replicate his <a href="/wiki/Uo_Uo_no_Mi,_Model:_Seiryu" title="Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu">Uo Uo no Mi, Model: Seiryu</a> Devil Fruit, although the <a href="/wiki/Artificial_Devil_Fruit" title="Artificial Devil Fruit">results</a> were noted to be unsatisfactory. The World Government wanted him to give the fruit to them, but Vegapunk considered it a failure and refused, leaving it on the island of <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard" title="Punk Hazard">Punk Hazard</a>.
</p><p>At some point, Vegapunk was with <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Borsalino</a> and while on a trip to deal with a bear attack, encountered a boy named <a href="/wiki/Sentomaru" title="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</a>, who had already defeated the bears. Sentomaru revealed he was kicked out of his village and requested a job to Vegapunk. Vegapunk acknowledged the boy's strength and agreed to hire him as his personal bodyguard.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">[98]</a></sup> Later on, Borsalino agreed to let Vegapunk study the ability of his <a href="/wiki/Pika_Pika_no_Mi" title="Pika Pika no Mi">Pika Pika no Mi</a> for a future <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">project</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">[99]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f6/Vegapunk_Visits_Elbaph.png/revision/latest?cb=20240317020848" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Visits Elbaph" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vegapunk Visits Elbaph.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Visits_Elbaph.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f6/Vegapunk_Visits_Elbaph.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240317020848"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f6/Vegapunk_Visits_Elbaph.png/revision/latest?cb=20240317020848" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Visits Elbaph" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f6/Vegapunk_Visits_Elbaph.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240317020848" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vegapunk Visits Elbaph.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Visits_Elbaph.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f6/Vegapunk_Visits_Elbaph.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240317020848"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vegapunk_Visits_Elbaph.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk visits Elbaph and its library of books salvaged from Ohara.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>22 years ago, Vegapunk would receive news of the <a href="/wiki/Ohara_Incident" title="Ohara Incident">Ohara Incident</a> at his lab in Punk Hazard, taking note of Robin's Wanted Poster.<sup id="cite_ref-c1120_50-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1120-50">[50]</a></sup> Several months later, Vegapunk took a trip to <a href="/wiki/Ohara" title="Ohara">Ohara</a> to pay his respects to the late Professor Clover. He came across the lake in the center of the island filled with books, and the realization that this was the final stand made by Ohara's scholars brought him to tears. Vegapunk noticed a group of <a href="/wiki/Giants" title="Giants">giants</a> pulling the books from the lake before being approached by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Monkey D. Dragon</a>, who had also come to pay his respects. Dragon explained to him that the giants were from <a href="/wiki/Elbaph" title="Elbaph">Elbaph</a>, and that they knew the value of the books. Dragon lamented Vegapunk's refusal to join the <a href="/wiki/Freedom_Fighters" title="Freedom Fighters">Freedom Fighters</a> due to lack of resources, but Vegapunk explained that he felt his abilities were put to better use with the World Government. Though he wished to take the books with him back to Punk Hazard, Vegapunk feared that his superiors would hear about the survival of Ohara's library, and so he entrusted them to the giants. Vegapunk later took a secret visit to Elbaph to read all of the rescued books in order to carry on the work of researching them. There, he met <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_D._Saul" title="Jaguar D. Saul">Jaguar D. Saul</a>, who had led the giants in salvaging the books.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">[100]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8b/Vegapunk_Dismisses_Caesar.png/revision/latest?cb=20221120153617" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Dismisses Caesar" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="199" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vegapunk Dismisses Caesar.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Dismisses_Caesar.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8b/Vegapunk_Dismisses_Caesar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221120153617"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8b/Vegapunk_Dismisses_Caesar.png/revision/latest?cb=20221120153617" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Dismisses Caesar" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8b/Vegapunk_Dismisses_Caesar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221120153617" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="199" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vegapunk Dismisses Caesar.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Dismisses_Caesar.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8b/Vegapunk_Dismisses_Caesar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20221120153617"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vegapunk_Dismisses_Caesar.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk tells Caesar that he is dismissed.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Four years prior to the current storyline, Vegapunk was leading chemical weapons tests in his lab on Punk Hazard. His former colleague, <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>, created an extremely <a href="/wiki/H2S" title="H2S">powerful chemical weapon</a>. When Vegapunk attempted to dismiss Caesar for his reckless behavior, Caesar retaliated by detonating that weapon, turning Punk Hazard into a wasteland.<sup id="cite_ref-c684_1-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c684-1">[1]</a></sup> The island was closed off after this incident and a <a href="/wiki/Dragon_Number_Thirteen" title="Dragon Number Thirteen">dragon that Vegapunk had created</a> was also abandoned. Since Vegapunk had been leading the experiments, he was blamed for the incident.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">[101]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Kuma_and_Bonney_meet_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126150316" class="image"><img alt="Kuma and Bonney meet Vegapunk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="222" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kuma and Bonney meet Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Kuma_and_Bonney_meet_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Kuma_and_Bonney_meet_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231126150316"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Kuma_and_Bonney_meet_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126150316" class="image"><img alt="Kuma and Bonney meet Vegapunk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Kuma_and_Bonney_meet_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231126150316" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="222" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kuma and Bonney meet Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Kuma_and_Bonney_meet_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Kuma_and_Bonney_meet_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231126150316"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kuma_and_Bonney_meet_Vegapunk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk meets Kuma and Bonney.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shortly after this event, Vegapunk was transferred to a new facility on <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a>, still under employment of the World Government, around this time Borsalino (promoted to <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> under the pseudonym of Kizaru), visited him and got a look at Vegapunk's blueprint work for Egghead's construction.<sup id="cite_ref-c1124_97-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1124-97">[97]</a></sup> At the suggestion of Dragon, <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> decided to take his daughter <a href="/wiki/Jewelry_Bonney" title="Jewelry Bonney">Jewelry Bonney</a> to see him in an attempt to cure her <a href="/wiki/Sapphire_Scales" title="Sapphire Scales">Sapphire Scales</a> disease. Vegapunk was surprised by Kuma's sudden appearance, but quickly moved past it. When Kuma asked Vegapunk if he could cure Bonney's disease, Vegapunk confirmed he could indeed cure her, and explained that he would perform a stem cell transplant. Vegapunk was then shocked to learn that Kuma was a <a href="/wiki/Buccaneers" title="Buccaneers">Buccaneer</a> after checking his blood, although he had not enough samples to answer Kuma's questions about his heritage. After discovering this fact, Vegapunk offered to waive the expenses for Bonney's transplant, as long as he was allowed to clone Kuma. Kuma was shocked at the offer, but accepted it nonetheless, as Bonney's safety was his top priority, leading to the creation of the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> human weapons.<sup id="cite_ref-c1099_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1099-46">[46]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c485_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c485-11">[11]</a></sup> 
</p><p>During his time with Kuma, Vegapunk was visited by Borsalino again, which put him on edge as he knew he was there with a Marine fleet to which Kizaru defended himself claiming he was just doing his job. Carrying a Den Den Mushi with <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a> on the line, he was not fond of his dealings with Kuma or him being used as the model for the Pacifista project; however, he relented on the condition that certain demands be made. The demands were that Kuma must become a <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a>, that he must become a human weapon for the government, and that his memories must be erased for total control. These conditions outraged Vegapunk and he argued that these conditions would effective Kuma; however, Kuma agreed with these conditions as it would be the only way he could save Bonney, bringing Vegapunk to tears and leaving Kizaru distraught. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Saturn_Negotiating_With_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20231207211339" class="image"><img alt="Saturn Negotiating With Kuma" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="133" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Saturn Negotiating With Kuma.png" data-image-key="Saturn_Negotiating_With_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Saturn_Negotiating_With_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231207211339"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Saturn_Negotiating_With_Kuma.png/revision/latest?cb=20231207211339" class="image"><img alt="Saturn Negotiating With Kuma" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Saturn_Negotiating_With_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231207211339" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="133" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Saturn Negotiating With Kuma.png" data-image-key="Saturn_Negotiating_With_Kuma.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/03/Saturn_Negotiating_With_Kuma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231207211339"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Saturn_Negotiating_With_Kuma.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk overhears Saturn's demands for Kuma's modifications and Bonney's cure.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Saturn asked Vegapunk how long it would take to cure the Sapphire Scales, to which he stated would be up to half a year and another full year for her to be able to go outside. Hearing this, Saturn decided to make Bonney a hostage and placed her under government watch, until Kuma's free will was completely erased. This angered Vegapunk again, arguing that both Kuma and Bonney would never be able to see each other again. Saturn brushed this off, saying that if this order is violated, Bonney would be made into a slave. While Kuma and Bonney went through with testing, Vegapunk began writing down his weapon ideas with even more ideas flowing through his head, wishing that there were five of him to keep up with his ideas. As the months went on, Vegapunk became close with Kuma and Bonney, eating pizza and partying with them, alongside Kizaru and Sentomaru, when they had the time. Vegapunk would also have Kizaru, Sentomaru, and Kuma help to construct more of the lab.<sup id="cite_ref-c1124_97-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1124-97">[97]</a></sup> Six months later, Vegapunk happily told Bonney that in one more year she would be able to go out into the sunlight and told Bonney she could come back to the lab after she was cured, with Kuma thanking him.<sup id="cite_ref-c1100_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1100-40">[40]</a></sup>
</p><p>About a year afterwards, Vegapunk had his large head surgically cut off and his brain removed and stored into <a href="/wiki/Punk_Records" title="Punk Records">Punk Records</a> and replaced the top of his head with an apple top head. While Kuma underwent his modifications, <a href="/wiki/Stussy" title="Stussy">Stussy</a> commented on Vegapunk's brain removal, while also pondering on if Kuma's fate of being a human with no will would be worse than a clone with a will, to which he replied that she was human. Kuma questioned what would happen if he lost his free will; Vegapunk answered that it would mean losing human emotions and memories, but ensured Kuma that he would have at least one more year to retain bare minimum of consciousness.<sup id="cite_ref-c1101_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1101-28">[28]</a></sup>
</p><p>Following the incident at <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a>, Vegapunk was at Egghead talking with Kuma about the Pacifista's augmentation going well and asked Kuma if he was aware of the <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">boy</a> who declared war on the World Government, causing Kuma to reveal to Vegapunk that he was Dragon's son. Vegapunk was surprised by this news and mused with Kuma over the similarities Luffy's powers had to <a href="/wiki/Nika" title="Nika">Nika</a>. During this time, he enlisted Kuma's help in researching memories since the <a href="/wiki/Nikyu_Nikyu_no_Mi" title="Nikyu Nikyu no Mi">Nikyu Nikyu no Mi</a>'s ability could make them tangible.<sup id="cite_ref-c1072_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1072-47">[47]</a></sup> With his research on Kizaru's Devil Fruit powers, Vegapunk managed to replicate them and manufacture functional and tangible laser beams that cause damage, becoming the only person in the world with the technological prowess.<sup id="cite_ref-Pacifistas_59-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pacifistas-59">[59]</a></sup> His attempts to replicate <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a> Devil Fruits resulted in the creation of <a href="/wiki/Green_Blood" title="Green Blood">Green Blood</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">[102]</a></sup> Prior to the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>, when the time came for Vegapunk to perform the final operation on Kuma, he argued with Saturn on implanting a self-destruct switch on Kuma and attempted to reason with Saturn on allowing bare minimum consciousness for him before the operation, but the elder refused. Kuma had overheard this and finished his original agreement with Vegapunk to use the Nikyu Nikyu no Mi's ability to create a copy of his memories to study, Vegapunk then tearfully proceeded with the operation of removing the last of Kuma's free will while various doctors and Sentomaru prayed for him.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">[103]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1102_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1102-31">[31]</a></sup> However, upon Kuma's request, Vegapunk programmed the mission to protect the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> into Kuma's memory banks.<sup id="cite_ref-c603_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c603-49">[49]</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point two years ago, Vegapunk managed to split his being into six satellites who shared his brain in order to help with his work. Together, they visited Mary Geoise at some point. While Vegapunk and most of his Satellites saw the <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Nobles</a>' cruelty as horrendous and looked down on them for it, little did they knew at the time that <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk/York" title="Vegapunk/York">York</a> secretly desired to become a Celestial Dragon herself, even if it meant betraying her peers.<sup id="cite_ref-c1078_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1078-38">[38]</a></sup>
</p><p>Three months prior to the <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Incident" title="Egghead Incident">Egghead Incident</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cipher_Pol#CP5" title="Cipher Pol">CP5</a> investigated Vegapunk for researching the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">[104]</a></sup>
</p><p>Prior to the <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a>, <a href="/wiki/Issho" title="Issho">Admiral Fujitora</a> met with Vegapunk, and the scientist revealed the <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">[105]</a></sup> which were the culmination of Vegapunk's research into cloning, cyborgs, Devil Fruits, and lunarians.<sup id="cite_ref-c1070p8_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1070p8-72">[72]</a></sup>
</p><p>About two weeks prior to the beginning of the Egghead Incident, Vegapunk, Shaka, Pythagoras discovered odd discrepancies in the Mother Flame's energy output. Shaka quickly deduced that the culprit logically must be one of the Vegapunks, and that the three of them were the only ones that had alibis. The three concluded that they would have to continue observing in order to get more information. One week later, Pythagoras revealed that he discovered the culprit to be York, citing that her memories uploaded to Punk Records were invalid, and that the Den Den Mushi recordings of the Mother Flame room were tampered with. Vegapunk was shocked by the news, and immediately assumed it to be Lilith, due to her apparent nature as his "evil". A day later, the <a href="/wiki/Lulusia_Kingdom" title="Lulusia Kingdom">Lulusia Kingdom</a> was obliterated through what Vegapunk assumed was an <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Weapons" title="Ancient Weapons">Ancient Weapon</a>. Shaka suggested fleeing Egghead, but Vegapunk reminded him of the World Government's influence over the entire planet, and that escape would be impossible. When Vegapunk explained that their deaths were imminent and likely inevitable, Shaka and Pythagoras fearlessly stated their intentions to join him in his plan to reveal their knowledge on the <a href="/wiki/Void_Century" title="Void Century">Void Century</a> to the world. Sometime later, Vegapunk would hide the Broadcast Den Den Mushi within the Iron Giant, pretending it to be nothing when questioned by York.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Vegapunks_Erase_Memories.png/revision/latest?cb=20240818150602" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunks Erase Memories" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vegapunks Erase Memories.png" data-image-key="Vegapunks_Erase_Memories.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Vegapunks_Erase_Memories.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240818150602"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Vegapunks_Erase_Memories.png/revision/latest?cb=20240818150602" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunks Erase Memories" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Vegapunks_Erase_Memories.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240818150602" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vegapunks Erase Memories.png" data-image-key="Vegapunks_Erase_Memories.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f0/Vegapunks_Erase_Memories.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240818150602"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vegapunks_Erase_Memories.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shaka, Pythagoras, and Stella prepare to erase their memories.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Two days before the beginning of the Egghead Incident, Shaka would assist Vegapunk in his recording, setting up the Den Den Mushi and expressing his frustration in Vegapunk wishing to wait so long to reveal his message. Realizing that their behavior would be perceived as strange by the other Vegapunks, the trio decided the best course of action would be to erase their memories, in order to ensure their plans would remain undiscovered. After doing so, the three read a message that Vegapunk had written just prior and were naturally shocked by the overload of information that they had just forgotten being revealed once again in such a short time.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">[106]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>While Vegapunk was working on a warping experiment, it backfired, and he got stuck inside the Iron Giant's armor. Luffy headed his way to help Vegapunk and freed him. Vegapunk then thanked him and recognized him as <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Dragon</a>'s son, knowing he would come to <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a>. However, he ended up flying too high in the air due to his boots and begged for help once more.<sup id="cite_ref-c1066_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1066-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Bonney_threatens_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240317021208" class="image"><img alt="Bonney threatens Vegapunk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bonney threatens Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Bonney_threatens_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Bonney_threatens_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240317021208"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Bonney_threatens_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240317021208" class="image"><img alt="Bonney threatens Vegapunk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Bonney_threatens_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240317021208" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bonney threatens Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Bonney_threatens_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Bonney_threatens_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240317021208"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bonney_threatens_Vegapunk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk is threatened by Bonney.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Vegapunk later explained to the group his background, his satellites and the meaning behind <a href="/wiki/Punk_Records" title="Punk Records">Punk Records</a>. as well as his ultimate goal to have a database everybody had access to. He was, though, confronted by an extremely angry Bonney, who demanded Vegapunk explain his reasons for turning her <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">father</a> into a cyborg, even threatening him with a beam saber she had found earlier. However, the saber attracted a horde of insects, and after she passed out, Vegapunk admitted to Luffy, Chopper, and <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> that he did not blame Bonney for hating him, well understanding of her resentment. However, he then added he had something he had wanted to give to her.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">[107]</a></sup>
</p><p>Vegapunk then excitedly explained to the group his ultimate goal of providing free energy for everybody around the world, mentioning the existence of an "ancient energy" that he believed was the Iron Giant's power source. However, because of his studies about said energy, he was fully aware he had uncovered too much of the past and that the Government wanted him dead, requesting Luffy to take him out to the sea with him and his crew. After Luffy agreed, Vegapunk told them to get to the Labophase, vanishing seconds later himself.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">[108]</a></sup> 
</p><p>It turned out Vegapunk had warped himself into the Labophase, appearing in the Observation Room where the other Satellites and the Straw Hats were observing Luffy's fight against Lucci. He then clarified the true nature of Luffy's Devil Fruit, mentioning that there was no such thing as a "Gomu Gomu no Mi". He marvelously observed Luffy's Gear 5 form and explained to the Straw Hats that this form resembled a god from the ancient texts, who was supposed to be a <a href="/wiki/Joy_Boy" title="Joy Boy">warrior of liberation</a> who would bring smiles to people, called <a href="/wiki/Nika" title="Nika">Nika</a>. Hearing that the Straw Hats never heard of this name, he explained to them that this name had been erased from history, but would always exist as long as people wished for him, concluding that all things were brought into the world with hope, including <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruits</a>. He then shared his theory about the existence of Devil Fruits with the Straw Hats, theorizing that every Devil Fruit was a possibility for human evolution that someone had desired beforehand. He concluded his theory by explaining that those with powers would exist in different dimensions dreamed up by someone else before them, leaving every single Straw Hat speechless at this theory.<sup id="cite_ref-c1069_41-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1069-41">[41]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Vegapunk then went on to explain to the Straw Hats how he was able to replicate Devil Fruits into <a href="/wiki/Artificial_Devil_Fruit" title="Artificial Devil Fruit">Artificial Fruits</a>, divulging that he could only so far recreate <a href="/wiki/Zoan" title="Zoan">Zoan</a> Devil Fruits, distancing himself from <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar</a>'s <a href="/wiki/SMILE" title="SMILE">SMILE</a> fruits by saying his process was vastly different and more acceptable than his. He then revealed that he had found a way of replicating <a href="/wiki/Paramecia" title="Paramecia">Paramecia</a> Devil Fruits by synthesizing the blood from a Paramecia User's Lineage Factor. Vegapunk concluded his explanation by stating that the Seraphim are the culmination of all his ideas, referring to them as "The Strongest Form of Humanity".<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">[109]</a></sup> 
</p><p>When Luffy's group later arrived at the Labophase, Vegapunk was chased by a furious Bonney who demanded that he reverse the <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a> modifications and turn her father back to normal, ignoring his pleas to listen to him. However, Vegapunk confessed that the process was irreversible, but he had a good reason for it.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">[110]</a></sup> Bonney, cunningly, turned herself into a child to divert Vegapunk's focus and, in a second of his carelessness, turned into a future version of herself and struck at him with <i>Distortion Future</i>. Vegapunk evaded her assault but was then successfully hit with <i>Toshi Tsuki</i>, turning him into a little child, unable to escape her grasp. She then once again demanded to know why Vegapunk took Kuma's personality from him, but Vegapunk once again replied he could not tell her due to a promise with Kuma. Bonney, however, was unsatisfied by this answer and angrily slammed the child-turned Vegapunk on the ground before turning her attention to a mysterious door. Vegapunk warned Bonney not to touch the bubble she had found there, but Bonney dismissed his words, throwing him off the room.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">[111]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Vegapunk_Imprisoned_in_Labophase.png/revision/latest?cb=20240609020644" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Imprisoned in Labophase" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vegapunk Imprisoned in Labophase.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Imprisoned_in_Labophase.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Vegapunk_Imprisoned_in_Labophase.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240609020644"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Vegapunk_Imprisoned_in_Labophase.png/revision/latest?cb=20240609020644" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Imprisoned in Labophase" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Vegapunk_Imprisoned_in_Labophase.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240609020644" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vegapunk Imprisoned in Labophase.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Imprisoned_in_Labophase.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f8/Vegapunk_Imprisoned_in_Labophase.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240609020644"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vegapunk_Imprisoned_in_Labophase.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk imprisoned alongside the captured Cipher Pol agents.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Vegapunk was then abducted<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">[112]</a></sup> and imprisoned deep within the Labophase along with the other <a href="/wiki/Cipher_Pol" title="Cipher Pol">Cipher Pol</a> agents who had disappeared after their visits to Egghead. He confessed to a CP5 member he had no idea they were locked up down here for so long, and also realized that their imprisonment was connected to his research into the <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Poneglyphs</a>, which had been leaked to the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">[113]</a></sup> Shaka eventually found Vegapunk, but was then shot in the head by York, leaving Vegapunk surprised.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">[114]</a></sup> Vegapunk became furious and asked her if she was the one who imprisoned the Cipher Pol agents, but York replied that she wanted to be a World Noble. Vegapunk became confused and asked York why she would want to be like them. York laughed in response, further adding that the world only needed one Vegapunk.<sup id="cite_ref-c1078_38-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1078-38">[38]</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point, Vegapunk was freed from captivity and reunited with Bonney near the PAW room. She then gifted her a sapphire necklace, apparently from Kuma, and clarified to her about his role in Kuma's transformation into a human weapon. Having learned the truth of what had happened, Bonney apologized to Vegapunk and happily accepted his gift.
</p><p>Vegapunk then returned to the Control Room with Bonney, where the Straw Hats and <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a> had gathered together after foiling York's plans.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">[115]</a></sup>  Upon hearing from Stussy that the Marines had surrounded Egghead, Vegapunk asked Nami about her <a href="/wiki/Log_Pose" title="Log Pose">Log Pose</a> while setting up a plan to escape to Elbaph. He planned to use the <a href="/wiki/Vegaforce-01" title="Vegaforce-01">Vegaforce-01</a> to fly the Thousand Sunny over the Marine blockade and assigned Lilith to be the robot's pilot. When he mentioned that the robot would fall outside of Egghead's airspace, Franky assured him that a Coup de Burst from the Thousand Sunny would guarantee an escape from the Marines. Since York had put a password on the Frontier Dome preventing anyone from escaping, however, Vegapunk, along with Edison and Atlas, began to crack her code.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">[116]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/Stussy_Saves_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20231016203827" class="image"><img alt="Stussy Saves Vegapunk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="187" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Stussy Saves Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Stussy_Saves_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/Stussy_Saves_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231016203827"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/Stussy_Saves_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20231016203827" class="image"><img alt="Stussy Saves Vegapunk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/Stussy_Saves_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231016203827" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="187" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Stussy Saves Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Stussy_Saves_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/Stussy_Saves_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231016203827"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Stussy_Saves_Vegapunk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Stussy protects Vegapunk.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While continuing to work on cracking the code, Vegapunk was alerted by Usopp that the Marines were beginning their assault. Vegapunk was confused by this, proclaiming that the island's defenses were nigh impenetrable. Upon realization that it was actually Kizaru on the island, Vegapunk felt terrible about Sentomaru having to fight him, and said it was alright for him to flee if he could not bring himself to do it. Sentomaru's defeat caused Vegapunk to break into tears, although he refused to give up on trying to get the barrier down. A moment later, as soon as Kizaru arrived in the Labophase, <a href="/wiki/Rob_Lucci" title="Rob Lucci">Rob Lucci</a> attempted to kill Vegapunk amidst the confusion. Stussy, who noticed just in time, quickly stepped in front of Vegapunk and took the attack in his place, promptly collapsing to the ground, but saving Vegapunk's life.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">[117]</a></sup>
</p><p>Her sacrifice later enabled Vegapunk to successfully crack the password and disable the Frontier Dome's defense system, celebrating alongside Atlas and Edison for doing so. Having done that, Vegapunk then contacted Franky, asking if the Vegaforce-01 had been brought into position, not knowing it had gotten destroyed by Kizaru. Much to everyone's horror, including Vegapunk, Kizaru later appeared in the Control Room to fulfill his mission, but before he could execute it, Kizaru was grabbed by a giant Luffy, much to Vegapunk's surprise.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">[118]</a></sup> When Atlas said she was going to leave to regain control of the Pacifista, Vegapunk wanted to come with her to save Bonney after finding out she was alive, despite being told that the Marines were after him. He contacted Franky and Sanji of the situation and the two decided to help him. Vegapunk and Atlas then left the Control Room in the Vegatank-08 to go rescue Bonney, with Vegapunk saying he would not leave her to die.<sup id="cite_ref-c1093_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1093-119">[119]</a></sup>
</p><p>Vegapunk entrusted Sanji to rescue Bonney before the tank could reach the Fabiriophase, and the group was successful in recovering her. As the group headed back up to the Labophase, they witnessed <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a>'s arrival. On the way down, Vegapunk requested that Sanji not defend him should he be attacked, to the latter's confusion. Vegapunk stated that his death would likely result in something huge taking place. He then brought up the topic of the One Piece to Sanji, telling him that he hoped the Straws Hats would be the ones to find it, adding even further to Sanji's bewilderment.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">[120]</a></sup> Kizaru then destroyed the clouds the Vegatank-08 was riding on, which sent it crashing onto the ground. Upon landing, Vegapunk's group was cornered by Saturn.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">[121]</a></sup> After Bonney tried to attack Saturn and was caught by him, Vegapunk's group tried to rescue her. However, they found themselves unable to move, which Vegapunk speculated was because of Saturn's Devil Fruit ability. They were forced to watch as the Marines raised their weapons to execute Bonney.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">[122]</a></sup> As Vegapunk was still unable to move, Saturn revealed to Bonney he was the one responsible for giving her and her mother <a href="/wiki/Ginny" title="Ginny">Ginny</a> Sapphire Scales due to a failed experiment. Vegapunk grew furious with Saturn for being the cause of tearing Kuma's family apart and hiding the disease under the guise of a bargaining deal, but Saturn dismissed this claiming he did not bother with the feelings of those beneath him. 
</p><p>When a Marine in the area notified Saturn that Kuma himself had arrived at the island, Vegapunk grew shocked as to why.<sup id="cite_ref-c1103_123-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1103-123">[123]</a></sup> After Kuma punched Saturn, Vegapunk thought to himself on how this was possible as the self-destruct switch he was forced to implant in Kuma would instead shut down his entire body, coming to the conclusion that it must have been a specific aspect of the <a href="/wiki/Buccaneers" title="Buccaneers">Buccaneers</a>. Saturn then questioned Vegapunk on how Kuma could move as he had activated the self-destruct command days ago, but Vegapunk did not elaborate further beyond claiming that it was the "power of love". Vegapunk then ordered Atlas to carry Kuma back to the Labophase, but Kizaru intervened. Disappointed about Kizaru's role in all this, Vegapunk spared no kind words to his "friend".<sup id="cite_ref-c1104_124-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1104-124">[124]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Vegapunk_Watches_Egghead_Destruction.png/revision/latest?cb=20240128150627" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Watches Egghead Destruction" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vegapunk Watches Egghead Destruction.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Watches_Egghead_Destruction.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Vegapunk_Watches_Egghead_Destruction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240128150627"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Vegapunk_Watches_Egghead_Destruction.png/revision/latest?cb=20240128150627" class="image"><img alt="Vegapunk Watches Egghead Destruction" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Vegapunk_Watches_Egghead_Destruction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240128150627" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vegapunk Watches Egghead Destruction.png" data-image-key="Vegapunk_Watches_Egghead_Destruction.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Vegapunk_Watches_Egghead_Destruction.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240128150627"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vegapunk_Watches_Egghead_Destruction.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Vegapunk witnesses the destruction of his work.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After hearing about the oncoming destruction of Egghead from a <a href="/wiki/Buster_Call" title="Buster Call">Buster Call</a>, Vegapunk begged Saturn and Kizaru to call it off, as destroying Egghead would cause severe scientific setbacks. Despite his pleas, his concerns were met with contempt from Saturn, and silence from Kizaru. Saturn then elected to inform Vegapunk that he had ordered the destruction of a vessel carrying Egghead researchers. Vegapunk was horrified at the news, and angrily told Saturn that said researchers had nothing to do with his Void Century research. Saturn once again rejected Vegapunk's concerns, instead telling him that it was his own fault that the current events were transpiring. Moments later, the Buster Call began, and Vegapunk silently watched as his years of research on Egghead were reduced to rubble via bombardment. To make matters worse, Kizaru prevented Vegapunk's allies from escaping while Saturn ordered the Pacifista to shoot them down. Vegapunk watched and remembered dwelling on this specific scenario, citing that the Pacifista may be clones of Kuma, but none of them cared about Bonney or Kuma's friends.<sup id="cite_ref-c1105_125-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1105-125">[125]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Saturn_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240204150225" class="image"><img alt="Saturn Stabs Vegapunk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="161" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Saturn Stabs Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Saturn_Stabs_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Saturn_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240204150225"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Saturn_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240204150225" class="image"><img alt="Saturn Stabs Vegapunk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Saturn_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240204150225" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="161" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Saturn Stabs Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Saturn_Stabs_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9f/Saturn_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240204150225"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Saturn_Stabs_Vegapunk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Saturn impales Vegapunk.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Knowing that he could not let the very idea of Kuma attacking Bonney become a reality, Vegapunk quickly ordered Atlas to inform Bonney of her special status in the command hierarchy. Upon learning of this, Bonney ordered the Pacifista to help them all escape Egghead, to which they responded by attacking the Marines. Vegapunk thought about his life decisions while this was occurring, acknowledging that giving Bonney the highest position in the command hierarchy was his single selfish decision in his employment by the World Government. He knew that this would have severe consequences, which came in the form of Saturn stabbing him through the back with one of his legs. Vegapunk collapsed to the ground, and moments later, Bonney came to his side to beg him to leave with them. While this was happening, Luffy arrived back fully reenergized and in his Gear 5 form. Vegapunk weakly told Bonney that Luffy was Nika, the very being that she, Kuma, and many others had been waiting for for hundreds of years.<sup id="cite_ref-c1106_126-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1106-126">[126]</a></sup> As Vegapunk laid on the ground from his injuries, Bonney told Luffy to avenge him by punching out Saturn, which he followed through on. Bonney then begged for Vegapunk to escape with her along with Atlas and Franky, but Vegapunk revealed to her that his injuries were nearly fatal and made it impossible for him to be moved without risking a worsening condition. Kizaru responded by attempting to shoot a laser at both Bonney and Vegapunk, but it was countered away by Sanji.<sup id="cite_ref-c1107_127-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1107-127">[127]</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Borsalino_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240225150415" class="image"><img alt="Borsalino Stabs Vegapunk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Borsalino Stabs Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Borsalino_Stabs_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Borsalino_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240225150415"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Borsalino_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest?cb=20240225150415" class="image"><img alt="Borsalino Stabs Vegapunk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Borsalino_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240225150415" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Borsalino Stabs Vegapunk.png" data-image-key="Borsalino_Stabs_Vegapunk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1f/Borsalino_Stabs_Vegapunk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240225150415"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Borsalino_Stabs_Vegapunk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kizaru delivers a lethal blow to Vegapunk.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Vegapunk relented on being forced to reveal Bonney's control over the Pacifista, and begged the Straw Hats to take care of her. While this happened, Luffy ordered Sanji to take Vegapunk away from the chaotic area as Saturn returned, now transformed into his full beast form. As they made their escape, Sanji was kicked away by Kizaru, who then dealt Vegapunk a lethal blow. As his heartbeat flatlined, a pre-recorded message activated within his Lab where he announced to the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a> that he was going to tell them a certain truth.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Postmortem">Postmortem</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Sanji kept hold of Vegapunk's corpse as he and the other Straw Hats headed to the <a href="/wiki/Giant_Warrior_Pirates" title="Giant Warrior Pirates">Giant Warrior Pirates</a>' ship in order to escape the island.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup> Following their escape from Egghead, Vegapunk's body was laid somewhere within the giants' ship.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">[130]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Legacy">Legacy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Vegapunk's death immediately triggered the airing of his planned broadcast message, which successfully aired across the entire world. During the broadcast, the world's population was told what Vegapunk knew of the Void Century: namely about the <a href="/wiki/Great_War" title="Great War">Great War</a> between <a href="/wiki/Joy_Boy" title="Joy Boy">Joy Boy</a> and the <a href="/wiki/First_Twenty" title="First Twenty">First Twenty</a>, and the usage of the <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Weapons" title="Ancient Weapons">Ancient Weapons</a> causing global sea levels to rise 200 meters. Vegapunk also shared that his Mother Flame had been used to power an Ancient Weapon and predicted that the destruction of Lulusia would trigger the same sea level rise; this prediction came to pass shortly before he died and thus vindicated his message. Vegapunk warned the world that it would sink into the sea soon and the Great War had not truly ended so long as the Ancient Weapons still existed.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup>
</p><p>In the climax of his message, Vegapunk shared his belief that whoever found the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a> would decide the fate of the world. This was shown to invigorate many pirates and further their ambition of finding <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>'s treasure; members of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>' crews were particularly energized. This also caused some <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> to be motivated to find the treasure first before any pirate could.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">[132]</a></sup> Ultimately though, not all of Vegapunk's message was heard due to the efforts of the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> to find and kill the transmitting <a href="/wiki/Den_Den_Mushi" title="Den Den Mushi">Den Den Mushi</a>; the broadcast briefly went offline while Vegapunk was talking about the <a href="/wiki/Clan_of_D." class="mw-redirect" title="Clan of D.">Clan of D.</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup> and permanently ended before its conclusion as Vegapunk was sharing something else about Joy Boy.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite the death of Vegapunk's main body, his brain and Punk Records remained functional. Shaka, Pythagoras, and Atlas were destroyed, while Edison and Lilith hid their survivals from York by disconnecting from Punk Records. Lilith escaped Egghead with the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Giant_Warrior_Pirates" title="Giant Warrior Pirates">Giant Warrior Pirates</a>, and set sail to <a href="/wiki/Elbaph" title="Elbaph">Elbaph</a> with them.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">[135]</a></sup> Edison was able to retrieve <a href="/wiki/Punk_Records" title="Punk Records">Punk Records</a> from York, and the destroyed satellites survived by reconvening into his body, which was reconstructed using spare parts from all of the satellites except York and Lilith.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the original Japanese, the names of Vegapunk's satellites are written with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/kanji" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:kanji">kanji</a> which have meanings that correspond with the aspects they embody. For example, Lilith's name is written as <ruby lang="ja"><rb>悪</rb><rp>（</rp><rt>リリス</rt><rp>）</rp></ruby>, with a kanji character that means "evil" while the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/furigana" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:furigana">furigana</a> gives the reading <i>Ririsu</i> or "Lilith". In the <a href="/wiki/VIZ_Media" title="VIZ Media">VIZ</a> translation, these meanings are presented similarly to epithets, such as "Lilith the Evil" and "Shaka the Good".
</p><p>In the FUNimation dub, Vegapunk is given a German accent, as a clear reference to Albert Einstein who is his based on.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Playable_Appearance">Playable Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Treasure_Cruise" title="One Piece Treasure Cruise">One Piece Treasure Cruise</a></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 170px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Einstein_tongue.png/revision/latest?cb=20221113181653" class="image"><img alt="Einstein tongue" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="170" height="211" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Einstein tongue.png" data-image-key="Einstein_tongue.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Einstein_tongue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20221113181653"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Einstein_tongue.png/revision/latest?cb=20221113181653" class="image"><img alt="Einstein tongue" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Einstein_tongue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20221113181653" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="170" height="211" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Einstein tongue.png" data-image-key="Einstein_tongue.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/43/Einstein_tongue.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20221113181653"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Einstein_tongue.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Albert Einstein, the man who Vegapunk seems to be visually inspired by.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Vegapunk's appearance with gray hair, a mustache and a large tongue may be inspired by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albert_Einstein" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Albert Einstein">Albert Einstein</a>, particularly the iconic photo of Einstein sticking his tongue out, albeit in a more exaggerated manner.
<ul><li>His epithet as being the world's smartest man could also be taken off of Einstein, who was said to be one of the greatest scientists ever to exist due to his many contributions and theories in science.</li>
<li>His brain being cut out of his head alludes to Einstein's brain being removed after his death for research.
<ul><li>The shape of his cut head may be inspired by the movie poster for the 1983 American black comedy film, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Man_with_Two_Brains" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Man with Two Brains">The Man with Two Brains</a></i>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Keeping with this theme, Vegapunk's English voice actor, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kent_Williams" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Kent Williams">Kent Williams</a>, portrays him with an exaggerated German accent, which is where Einstein was from.</li></ul></li>
<li>The apple-like lid over Vegapunk's head may be a reference to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Newton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Isaac Newton">Isaac Newton</a> and the popular myth of an apple falling on his head, leading to the discovery of gravity.
<ul><li>Furthermore, his apple-like head may also be a reference to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/tree_of_the_knowledge_of_good_and_evil" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:tree of the knowledge of good and evil">tree of the knowledge of good and evil</a> from the Bible, in which many media and sources depicted its fruit as an apple.</li>
<li>It could also be a reference to the fact in many pieces of media young students would usually give their teacher an apple as a sign of respect.</li></ul></li>
<li>Vegapunk's goal of providing the world with free energy could be a reference to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nikola_Tesla" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nikola Tesla">Nikola Tesla</a>, who also wanted to provide free energy to the world.</li>
<li>Vegapunk seems to be somewhat themed around <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Astronomical_object" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Astronomical object">astronomical objects</a>, as his main body is known as the "Stella" (Latin for "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/star" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:star">star</a>") while his being is split into six additional people known as "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Natural_satellite" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Natural satellite">satellites</a>". The "Vega-" portion of his name may be derived from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vega" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vega">Vega</a>, the brightest star in the constellation of Lyra. In addition, his verbal tic contains the word "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/quasar" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:quasar">quasar</a>".</li>
<li>The reason Vegapunk's satellites are referred to using the kanji for "cat" is because <a href="/wiki/Kaku" title="Kaku">Kaku</a> uses the Japanese idiom "Neko no te mo kari tai"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">猫の手も借りたい</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> which literally means "I would want to borrow even a hand of a cat" and is commonly used to express that one is extremely busy.</li>
<li>The "Ibel Peace Prize" Vegapunk is shown being awarded <a href="/wiki/Germa_66%27s_Ahh..._An_Emotionless_Excursion" title="Germa 66's Ahh... An Emotionless Excursion">in his past</a> as a <a href="/wiki/MADS" title="MADS">MADS</a> scientist is based on the real life <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nobel_Peace_Prize" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nobel Peace Prize">Nobel Peace Prize</a>.
<ul><li>The "GP Flowers" scientific achievement that bestowed Vegapunk this award is likely a reference to the famous <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Flower_Power_(photograph)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Flower Power (photograph)">Flower Power</a> photograph taken during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/March_on_the_Pentagon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:March on the Pentagon">March on the Pentagon</a>, an event symbolic to the end of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vietnam_War" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Before he cut off the top of his head, Vegapunk used to wash his enlarged head by dipping it in a pool of <a href="/wiki/Scrubfish" class="mw-redirect" title="Scrubfish">scrubfish</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup></li>
<li>One of Vegapunk's inventions, the DOM Shoes, is a reference to the <a href="https://gundam.fandom.com/wiki/MS-09_Dom" class="extiw" title="w:c:gundam:MS-09 Dom">MS-09 Dom</a> <a href="https://gundam.fandom.com/wiki/Mobile_Weapon%23Mobile_Suit" class="extiw" title="w:c:gundam:Mobile Weapon">mobile suit</a>, as well as its many variants and successors, from the <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gundam" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Gundam">Gundam</a></i> franchise. Both the mobile suits and the DOM Shoes share their signature capability to hover/"fly".</li>
<li>Vegapunk's favorite foods are apple pie, coffee and macaroni spaghetti.<sup id="cite_ref-vc_9-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc-9">[9]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FVegapunk%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="width:auto; max-height: 230px; overflow:auto; margin-bottom:3px; padding-left:0.5em; border:1px solid #AAAAAA; -moz-border-radius-topleft:0.5em; -webkit-border-top-left-radius:0.5em; border-top-left-radius:0.5em;">
<span style="font-size:x-small"><div class="mw-references-wrap mw-references-columns"><ol class="references">
